Provides Fiscal 2026 Outlook</font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%;padding-left:5.5pt">Revenues increased 7% to $20.6 billion for the year&#59; 7% organic constant currency</font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%;padding-left:5.5pt">Employer Services new business bookings increased 3% for the year to $2.1 billion</font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%;padding-left:5.5pt">Net earnings increased 9% to $4.1 billion for the year, and adjusted net earnings increased 8% to $4.1 billion</font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%;padding-left:5.5pt">Adjusted EBIT increased 9% to $5.3 billion for the year, and adjusted EBIT margin increased 50 basis points to 26.0% </font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%;padding-left:5.5pt">Diluted earnings per share (&#34;EPS&#34;) increased 10% to $9.98 for the year&#59; adjusted diluted EPS increased 9% to $10.01</font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%;padding-left:5.5pt">Fiscal 2026 consolidated outlook includes revenue growth of 5% to 6%, adjusted EBIT margin expansion of 50 to 70 basis points, and adjusted diluted EPS growth of 8% to 10%</font></div><div style="text-indent:9pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:138%">ROSELAND, N.J. &#8211; July&#160;30, 2025</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%"> &#8211; ADP (Nasdaq&#58; ADP), a global leader in HR and payroll solutions, today announced its fourth quarter and fiscal 2025 financial results and provided its fiscal 2026 outlook.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:138%">Fourth Quarter and Fiscal 2025 Consolidated Results</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">Compared to last year&#8217;s fourth quarter, revenues increased 8% to $5.1 billion and 6% on an organic constant currency basis. Net earnings increased 10% to $911 million, and adjusted net earnings increased 8% to $923 million. Adjusted EBIT increased 9% to $1.2 billion, representing an adjusted EBIT margin increase of 40 basis points in the quarter to 23.7%. ADP&#8217;s effective tax rate for the quarter was 23.5% on both a reported basis and an adjusted basis. Diluted EPS increased 10% to $2.23, and adjusted diluted EPS increased 8% to $2.26.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">For the full year, revenues increased 7% to $20.6 billion, 7% organic constant currency. Net earnings increased 9% to $4.1 billion, and adjusted net earnings increased 8% to $4.1 billion. Adjusted EBIT increased 9% to $5.3 billion, resulting in adjusted EBIT margin expansion of 50 basis points to 26.0%. ADP's full year effective tax rate was 23.2% on both a reported and adjusted basis. Diluted EPS increased 10% to $9.98, and adjusted diluted EPS increased 9% to $10.01, including a net share count reduction.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">&#34;We concluded fiscal year 2025 with strong revenue and earnings growth,&#34; stated Maria Black, President and Chief Executive Officer, ADP. &#34;Revenue growth in our Employer Services and PEO segments came in at the high-end of our full year expectations, bolstered by record-high client satisfaction levels across the company. As we enter a new fiscal year, we remain committed to actively listening to our clients and consistently meeting their needs through cutting-edge products, premium services, and exceptional experiences designed to elevate the world of work.&#34;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">&#8220;Solid execution and our resilient business model allowed us to produce strong results for the fiscal year,&#8221; said Peter Hadley, Chief Financial Officer, ADP. &#8220;As we look ahead to fiscal 2026, our focus is on delivering consistently strong revenue growth and continued margin expansion to drive healthy returns for our shareholders.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="height:42.75pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">1</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:42.75pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">Adjusted EBIT, adjusted EBIT margin, adjusted net earnings, adjusted diluted earnings per share, adjusted effective tax rate and organic constant currency are all non-GAAP financial measures. var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
